JAP_foreign_policy_category = {
	TNO_jamaica_antiimperialist_propaganda = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_JAP_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		cost = 20

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		days_remove = 14
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_chance_low = yes
			TNO_increase_foreign_intervention_low = yes
		}
	}


	TNO_jamaica_promote_black_power = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_nationalism

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_JAP_interventions_not_blocked = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { GDP > 0 } }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_50_million

		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes
			TNO_increase_foreign_intervention_low = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_court_JLP_leaders_cost
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.05 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
		}
	}



	TNO_jamaica_fabricate_claims = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_political_action

		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_foreign_intervention > 75 }
			}
		}

		cost = 35

		fire_only_once = no
		days_re_enable = 0

		complete_effect = {
			TNO_increase_jamaica_indep_chance_med = yes
			TNO_increase_foreign_intervention_med = yes
		}
	}

	TNO_jamaica_help_rastafarians = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_document_target

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_jamaican_referendum_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			TNO_JAP_interventions_not_blocked = yes
			TNO_us_intervention_medium_foreign = yes
		}

			factor = 1000
		}

		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 14.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp

		days_remove = 7
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_re_enable = 0

		remove_effect = {
			USA = {
				country_event = { id = wif_crisis.15 }
			}

			TNO_decrease_jamaica_indep_daily_tick_low = yes

	}

		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_jamaica_crisis_intervention_blocked
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 500
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { WIN.WIN_foreign_intervention < 80 }
			}
		}
	}



	TNO_jamaica_americans_investigation_jap = {

JAP_foreign_policy_category = {
	TNO_jamaica_crisis_restoring_order_jap = {
		priority = 10
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_propaganda
		activation = {
			check_variable = { WIN.WIN_fervor < 10.1 }
			WIN = { has_country_flag = Jamaica_Crisis_Unresolved }
		}
		available = {
			TNO_jamaica_crisis_fervor_not_low = yes
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 7
		days_remove = 1

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = TNO_jamaica_crisis_restoring_order_effect
			# US side handles consequences
		}
	}

	TNO_smuggle_honduran_guns = {

#################################
## West African Conflict (WAC) ##
#################################


JAP_foreign_policy_category = {

	# Stabotage Decisions

	JAP_distribute_weapons_to_partisans = {
		# Reduce garrison strength for PP and guns
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_arms_crate
		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
			USA = { has_country_flag = USA_In_The_WAC_WAR }
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 80

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_inf_eq_check = 400 }
			check_variable = {
				var = num_equipment@infantry_equipment
				value = t_inf_eq_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check = 30 }
			check_variable = {
				var = political_power
				value = t_pp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_pp_inf_eq_dynamic

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -400
				}
				add_political_power = -30
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			USA = {
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -7.5 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_share_intelligence_on_american_bases = {
		# Reduce garrison strength for PP and cp
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_investigate
		fire_only_once = no

		visible = {

				var = political_power
				value = t_pp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = 10 }
			check_variable = {
				var = command_power
				value = t_cp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_political_power = -20
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			USA = {
				set_temp_variable = { tempWACGarrisonStrength = -7.5 }
				USA_change_wac_garrison_strength = yes
			}
		}
	}

	# Christmas Offensive
	JAP_WAC_prepare_offensive_campaign_mission = {
	# planning mission, when finished offensive is launched
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_border_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = JAP
		}
		priority = 200
		days_mission_timeout = 90
		is_good = yes
		fire_only_once = yes

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}
		activation = { always = no }

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision complete JAP_WAC_prepare_offensive_campaign_mission"
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: decision timeout JAP_WAC_prepare_offensive_campaign_mission"
			# launch event
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_WAC_prepare_offensive_campaign_mission_tt
			clr_country_flag = JAP_WAC_preparing_campaign
			clr_country_flag = JAP_WAC_preparing_campaign_action
			hidden_effect = {
				USA = {
					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = WEST_AFRICA_JAP_offensive_campaign
						days = JAP.WAC_camapaign_duration
					}
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.53
					}
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = global.west_african_nations
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								original_tag = FFR
								is_in_faction_with = FFR
							}
						}
						add_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = WEST_AFRICA_JAP_offensive_campaign
							days = WAC_camapaign_duration
						}
					}
				}
				JAP = { # clear variables
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.45
						days = WAC_camapaign_duration
					}
				}

				every_country = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					news_event = { id = west_african_crisis_news.27 days = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_WAC_toggle_infantry_equipment_shipments = {
		icon = {
			key = GFX_decision_generic_visibility_closed
			trigger = {
				has_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = GFX_decision_generic_visibility
			trigger = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible }
			}
		}
		priority = 30
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
			NOT = { is_ai = yes }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_WAC_toggle_infantry_equipment_shipments"
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible }
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_tt_1
				clr_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_tt_2
				set_country_flag = WAC_infantry_equipment_shipments_visible
			}
		}
	}

				type = support_equipment
				amount = 700

		}

		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }

		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes

		days_remove = 40

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.1
			stability_weekly= -0.002
			war_support_weekly = -0.002
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { check_variable = { JAP_WAC_divisions > 9 } }
				}
				add_to_variable = { JAP_advisor_level = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { target = CAO }
				TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
			}

			TNO_improve_conscription_policy_effectiveness_med = yes
			add_to_variable = { JAP_WAC_divisions = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				TNO_improve_conscription_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
				if = {
					limit = { OR = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1 has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3 } }
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.210
						days = 30
					}
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.211
						days = 66
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2 }

	JAP_send_military_advisors_WA = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 180
		days_remove = 30
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 24.99
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_25_pp
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_send_military_advisors_WA"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_political_power = -25
				if = {
					limit = { OR = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1 has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3 } }
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.202
						days = 30
					}
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.203
						days = 66
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_2 }
					country_event = {
						id = west_african_crisis.206
						days = 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = CAO }
				add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_military_advisors days = 180 }
			}
			CAO = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CAO_ACA }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = CAO_ACA
						add_idea = CAO_ACA_2
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_idea = CAO_ACA_2 }
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = CAO_ACA_2
						add_idea = CAO_ACA_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_promote_rebellion_WA = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_revolt
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_wac_selected = yes
		}

		days_re_enable = 74
		days_remove = 30
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			has_political_power > 24.99
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_25_pp
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_promote_rebellion_WA"
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_political_power = -25
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = FFR }
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = FFR }
					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_resistance
						days = 60
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_1
						has_global_flag = WAC_scenario_3
					}
					NOT = { country_exists = FFR }
					country_exists = WOL
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_in_faction_with = WOL }

					add_timed_idea = {
						idea = WEST_AFRICA_idea_resistance
						days = 60
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_ship_oil_WA = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_oil_extraction

				add_command_power = -5

JAP_foreign_policy_category = {

	JAP_OC_increase_commitment = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_prepare_civil_war
		visible = {
			tag = JAP
			TNO_fopo_baathism_support_selected = yes
			TNO_volunteer_cap_less_5 = yes
			check_variable = {
				JAP_OC_volunteer_sent < 3
			}
		}

		cost = 50
		days_re_enable = 21

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_OC_increase_commitment"
			add_command_power = 25

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.OIL_supported_by_JAP

				JAP = {
					set_temp_variable = { target = PREV }
					TNO_increase_volunteer_cap_1 = yes
				}
			}

			add_to_variable = {
				JAP_OC_volunteer_sent = 1
			}

			custom_effect_tooltip = OIL_USA_increase_volunteers_1 #reusing the usa tooltip

			add_to_variable = {
				JAP_OC_participation = 8
				tooltip = BOR_OC_add_participation
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = JAP_OC_participation min = 0 max = 100 }

		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
	}

	JAP_OC_bomb_someone = {

				add_political_power = -25
			}

				add_timed_idea = { idea = JAP_military_advisors days = 180 }
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_Aerial_and_Naval_Patrols = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_aircraft_carrier
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 0 }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { t_pp_check = 15 }
			check_variable = {
				var = command_power
				value = t_cp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = political_power
				value = t_pp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_pp_dynamic

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -5
				add_political_power = -15
				country_event = { id = JAP_ICW.202 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tempEscalation = 5 }
			INS_ICW_change_escalation = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { has_war_with = INS }
					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.05 }
					INS_ICW_modify_recon_factor = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				INS = {
					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.05 }
					INS_ICW_modify_recon_factor = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

						target = BKB
					}

						target = SLS
					}
				}
			}
			else = {

					target = INS
				}
			}
		}

	JAP_Authorise_Naval_Bombardment = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_battleship
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 1 }
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = JAP_INS_bombing_campaigns_tt
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_INS_is_doing_naval_bombardment }

		}

		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = SRB
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = SRB }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = MKS
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = MKS }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = BKB
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = BKB }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = NII
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = NII }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = SLS
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = SLS }
						}
					}
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = INS
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = INS }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = SRB
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = SRB }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = MKS
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = MKS }
						}
						AND = {
							is_owned_by = BKB
							NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = BKB }
						}
					}
					is_coastal = yes
				}
			}
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only


		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 4.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_5_cp
		days_remove = 30

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -5 }
			set_country_flag = JAP_INS_is_doing_naval_bombardment
			FROM = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { navy_bombardment }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = JAP_INS_is_doing_naval_bombardment
			FROM = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					static_modifiers = { navy_bombardment }
					province = { all_provinces = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_Authorise_Expanded_CAS = {
	icon = GFX_decision_generic_bombing
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 1 }
		}
		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = JAP_INS_bombing_campaigns_tt
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = JAP_INS_not_exceeded_bombing_limit
				check_variable = { JAP_INS_bombings < JAP_INS_max_bombings }
			}
		}

		state_target = yes
		target_trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					INS = {
						has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					is_core_of = INS
					NOT = { is_owned_by = JAP }
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = SRB
						is_fully_controlled_by = MKS
						is_fully_controlled_by = BKB
						is_fully_controlled_by = NII
						is_fully_controlled_by = SLS
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				FROM = {
					is_core_of = INS
					NOT = { is_owned_by = JAP }
					NOT = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = INS
						is_fully_controlled_by = SRB
						is_fully_controlled_by = MKS
						is_fully_controlled_by = BKB
					}
				}
			}
		}
		on_map_mode = map_only


		custom_cost_trigger = { command_power > 9.99 }
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp
		days_remove = 30

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_INS_bombings = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_INS_unresitricted_bombing }
				}
				FROM = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { targeted_bombing_campaign }
						province = { all_provinces = yes }
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_INS_unresitricted_bombing
				}
				FROM = {
					add_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { bombing_campaign }
						province = { all_provinces = yes }
					}
					damage_building = {
						type = infrastructure
						damage = 1
					}
				}
			}

		}
		remove_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { JAP_INS_bombings = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = JAP_INS_unresitricted_bombing }
				}
				FROM = {
					remove_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { targeted_bombing_campaign }
						province = { all_provinces = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = JAP_INS_unresitricted_bombing
				}
				FROM = {
					remove_province_modifier = {
						static_modifiers = { bombing_campaign }
						province = { all_provinces = yes }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_Anti_Bandit_Operations = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_use_force
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_indonesia_selected = yes
			check_variable = { global.ICW_phase > 2 }
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 150
		}

		days_remove = 30

		custom_cost_trigger = {
			set_temp_variable = { t_inf_eq_check = 600 }
			set_temp_variable = { t_cp_check = 10 }
			check_variable = {
				var = num_equipment@infantry_equipment
				value = t_inf_eq_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = command_power
				value = t_cp_check
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_cp_inf_eq_dynamic

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -10
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = infantry_equipment
					amount = -600
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tempDiscontent = 10 }
			INS_ICW_change_discontent = yes
			set_temp_variable = { tempEscalation = 10 }
			INS_ICW_change_escalation = yes
		}

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_Anti_Bandit_Operations_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						INS = {
							has_country_flag = INS_lubis_duumvirate
						}
					}
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = INS
						}
						every_controlled_state = {
							limit = {
								has_resistance = yes
							}
							add_compliance = 7.5
							add_resistance = -7.5
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_country = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction_with = INS
						}
						every_controlled_state = {
							limit = {
								has_resistance = yes
							}
							add_compliance = 7.5
							add_resistance = -7.5
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

					}

					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.075 }
					INS_ICW_modify_army_morale_factor = yes
					set_temp_variable = { v = 0.1 }
					INS_ICW_modify_recon_factor = yes
				}

		}

	JAP_PHI_morale_rises = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ignite_civil_war
		activation = {
			has_global_flag = PHI_proxy_war
			check_variable = { JAP_PHI_Morale_Rises_counter < 5 }
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}

		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 30

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_PHI_morale_rises_tt
			add_to_variable = { PHI.PHI_listless_spirit_army_org_factor = 0.06 }
			add_to_variable = { PHI.PHI_listless_spirit_dig_in_factor = 0.04 }
			add_to_variable = { PHI.PHI_listless_spirit_attack = 0.04 }
			add_to_variable = { PHI.PHI_listless_spirit_defence = 0.01 }
			add_to_variable = { JAP_PHI_Morale_Rises_counter = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { JAP_PHI_Morale_Rises_counter < 5 }
					}
					activate_mission = JAP_PHI_morale_rises
				}
				else = {
					remove_mission = JAP_PHI_morale_rises
					PHI = { country_event = { id = PHI_Blitz.0 days = 30 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = PHI_Doing_Reconstruction }
		}
		ai_will_do = {

		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_political_power > 9.99
			}
		}

		days_remove = 14
		fixed_random_seed = no

		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = { add_political_power = -10 }
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.02 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
			set_country_flag = PHI_Doing_Reconstruction
		}
		remove_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = PHI_Doing_Reconstruction
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var < 100 } }

				set_temp_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_temp = 10 }
				TNO_PHI_Reconstruction_Progress_Change = yes
				PHI = {
					set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_percentage = 0.03 }
					econ_GDP_boost_once_percentage = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				PHI = {
					set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_GDP_boost_percentage = 0.05 }
					econ_GDP_boost_once_percentage = yes
				}
			}
		}

	JAP_PHI_recon_timeout = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_philippines_war_selected = yes
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		is_good = no
		days_mission_timeout = 180
		selectable_mission = no
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = PHI_ideology
						option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_FAILED_RECONSTRUCTION
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 0 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PHI_ideology
							option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_PAREDES
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PHI_ideology
							option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_RECTO
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = PHI_ideology
							option = PHI_IDEOLOGY_OSMENA
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { PHI_reconstruction_var = 100 }
				}
				PHI_reconstruction_complete = yes
			}
			else = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_PHI_recon_timeout_tt
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = PHI_Blitz.24 days = 1 } }
				TNO_fopo_remove_philippines_reconstruction_tab = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

		ai_will_do = {

			modifier = { # Prevent CA_Conference_days_left from increasing endlessly due to CCP
				factor = 0

						option = CA_CONFERENCE_JAP

					}

			}
		}

		days_re_enable = 50

					}

	JAP_blow_it_up = {
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		visible = {
			is_in_array = { TNO_active_conflicts = token:GC_Turkestan }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes
		fire_only_once = yes
		days_mission_timeout = 500

		timeout_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: JAP_blow_it_up mission timer elapsed"
			TRK = {
				country_event = CA_TK_skeleton.28
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GER = {
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_ID = 22 }
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_Outcome = 2 }
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_Points = -50 }
					Cold_War_GUI_ManipulateVictory = yes
				}
				JAP = {
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_ID = 22 }
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_Outcome = 4 }
					set_temp_variable = { Victory_Points = 50 }
					Cold_War_GUI_ManipulateVictory = yes
				}
				set_global_flag = TNO_TURKES_KENES_OVER_OVER
				set_global_flag = TK_JAP_Victory
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					news_event = {
						id = WORLD.30052
					}
				}
				TAJ = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_leader = {
									character = TAJ_Mawlawi_Hindustoni
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
						}
						Tajikistan_Regime_Change_A1 = yes
					}
				}
				KYR = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_country_leader = {
									character = KYR_Turdakun_Usulbaliev
									ruling_only = yes
								}
							}
						}
						Kyrgyzstan_Regime_Change_A1 = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						dismantle_faction = yes
					}
					create_faction = Central_Asia_Defense_League
					set_country_flag = CADL_MEMBER
					add_to_faction = TAJ
					TAJ = { set_country_flag = CADL_MEMBER }
				}
				USA = {
					TNO_fopo_remove_ca_conference_tab = yes
				}
				GER = {
					TNO_fopo_remove_ca_conference_tab = yes
				}
				TNO_fopo_remove_ca_conference_tab = yes
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Mission JAP_blow_it_up Completed"
		}
	}

		}

				factor = 0.1
				check_variable = { global.Madagascar_JAP_influence > 64 }
			}
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = { check_variable = { global.Madagascar_JAP_influence > 10 } }
		custom_cost_text = MAD_CW_CCT_Faction
		days_re_enable = 14

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_utilize_guerrilla_tactics"
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_utilize_guerrilla_tactics_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { TEMP_MADCW_Factionalism = 10 }
				MAD_adjust_JAP_factionalism = yes
				var:Madagascar_selected_city = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { is_controlled_by = MAD }
						}

						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Limited_Authority }
							}
							remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Limited_Authority }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Hostile_Territory }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Tamed_Territory }
							}
							remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Tamed_Territory }
							add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAD_Limited_Authority }
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	JAP_ai_state_shift = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_ofn_stationing

				10 = {

				10 = {

##		Colombian Civil War (COL,CLC,CLL)      ##

### Border War Stage ###
JAP_foreign_policy_category = {
	JAP_hike_up_military_terrain_support = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_border_war
		available = {
			CLC = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = COL_double_interference_check
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = IBR_COL_bribing_officials
						has_country_flag = CLL_block_foreign_support
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_border_clashes_happening
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_15_cp
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 90

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_hike_up_military_terrain_support"
			add_command_power = -15

			CLC = {
				set_temp_variable = { CLC_Japanese_Support_Jungle_Temp = 0.03 }
				JAP_add_support_new_granada = yes
			}
		}
	}
	JAP_send_more_drill_instructors = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		available = {
			CLC = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = COL_double_interference_check
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = IBR_COL_bribing_officials
						has_country_flag = CLL_block_foreign_support
					}
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_border_clashes_happening
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 9.99
			has_political_power > 24.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp_25_pp
		days_remove = 7
		days_re_enable = 60

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_send_more_drill_instructors"
			add_command_power = -10
			add_political_power = -25

			CLC = {
				set_temp_variable = { CLC_Japanese_Support_Training_Temp = 0.03 }
				JAP_add_support_new_granada = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
### Civil War Preparations ###
JAP_foreign_policy_category = {
	JAP_COL_reorganize_the_army = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_military_parade
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_civil_war_preperations
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 9.99
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_10_cp
		days_remove = 90

		modifier = {
			army_org = 10
			breakthrough_factor = 0.05
			max_planning = 0.15
		}

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_COL_reorganize_the_army"
			hidden_effect = { add_command_power = -10 }
		}
	}
	JAP_COL_build_destroyed_infra = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_infrastructure
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_civil_war_preperations
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}
		cost = 35
		days_remove = 20
		fire_only_once = yes

		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_COL_build_destroyed_infra"
		}
		remove_effect = {
			1654 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 5
				}
				set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.025 }
				econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
			}
			1653 = {
				set_building_level = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
				}
				set_temp_variable = { state_value_multiplier_temp = 1.025 }
				econ_state_value_change_multiply_specified_state = yes
			}
		}
	}

			if = {
				limit = { CLC = { owns_state = 1700 } }

						type = bunker

						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
							limit_to_border = yes
						}
						level < 2
					}
				}
				1662 = {
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 2
						province = {
							all_provinces = yes
							limit_to_border = yes
						}
						level < 2
					}
				}

						type = bunker
						level = 2

							all_provinces = yes
							limit_to_border = yes

							type = bunker
							level = 2
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes
								limit_to_border = yes
							}
							level < 2
						}
					}

						set_building_level = {
							type = bunker
							level = 2
							province = {
								all_provinces = yes

							}

	JAP_COL_civil_war_countdown = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_clock
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_civil_war_preperations
		}
		activation = {
			always = no
		}
		available = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				always = no
			}
		}
		days_mission_timeout = var:COL.COL_civil_war_countdown
		selectable_mission = no

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = COL_civil_war_countdown_tt
		}
	}
	JAP_COL_bribe_COL_officials = {
		allowed = { original_tag = JAP }
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_money
		visible = {
			TNO_fopo_colombian_civil_war_selected = yes
			has_global_flag = COL_border_clashes_happening
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = JAP_block_foreign_support
			}
		}
		days_remove = 60
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			command_power > 14.99
			has_political_power > 14.99
			check_variable = { GDP > 0 }
		}
		custom_cost_text = decision_cost_25_million_15_cp_15_pp
		days_re_enable = 120


		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_COL_bribe_COL_officials"
			COL = {
				set_country_flag = JAP_COL_bribing_officials
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_COL_bribe_COL_officials_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				add_command_power = -15
				add_political_power = -15
				set_temp_variable = { removed_from_reserves = money_reserves }
				clamp_temp_variable = { var = removed_from_reserves min = 0 max = 0.025 }
				set_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = 0.025 }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { to_add_to_debt = removed_from_reserves }
				add_to_variable = { national_debt = to_add_to_debt }
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			COL = {
				clr_country_flag = JAP_COL_bribing_officials
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			base = 30
		}
	}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision JAP_COL_instruct_doctrine"
			hidden_effect = {
				army_experience = -10
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
				name = land_doc_bonus
				cost_reduction = 0.30
				uses = 1
				category = land_doctrine
			}
		}
	}
	JAP_COL_send_advisors = {

					idea = CLC_Japanese_advisors
					days = 90
				}
			}
		}
	}
